id=\"about\"><header data-slot=\"panel-header\" class=\"screen-line-bottom px-4 has-data-[slot=panel-description]:*:data-[slot=panel-title]:screen-line-bottom\"><h2 data-slot=\"panel-title\" class=\"font-heading text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight\"><span>Up early?</span></h2></header><div data-slot=\"panel-body\" class=\"p-4\"><div data-slot=\"prose\" class=\"prose max-w-none prose-syedmoin prose-zinc dark:prose-invert\"><ul>\n<li>I obsess over the <strong>small details</strong>: the spacing, the timing of an animation, the empty states and edge cases most people skip. To me, that polish is the whole point.</li>\n<li>I love the moment a hard problem finally clicks. I will happily sit with something until it makes sense, then make it look effortless.</li>\n<li>I build for the <strong>person on the other side of the screen</strong>. If something feels confusing or slow, I do not call it done.</li>\n<li>I lean toward <strong>simple and reliable</strong> over clever and fragile. The best solution is usually the one that still makes sense six months later.</li>\n<li>I stay genuinely <strong>curious</strong>. A lot of my growth comes from breaking things, reading how other people solved them, and quietly trying again.</li>\n<li>I care about <strong>finishing</strong>. I would rather do one thing properly than leave five half-built.</li>\n<li>Coffee, a good playlist, and a quiet hour are when my best work tends to happen.</li>\n</ul></div></div></section><section
